 Other parties, including the state's main opposition party Samajwadi Party, have questioned the intention of the Yogi government

 It is being said that a step was taken to implement this stringent law to target a particular community
 kya muslimon ke khilaaf he kanoon?upicoca (uttarapradesh control of argenised krime act) ke tahat sangathit rup main hone vaale aparaadh ko nishaanaa banaaya jayega
 Under this law, the person arrested will not be able to get bail before 6 months
 aaropee kii police remand 30 din ke liye lee ja sakati he, jabaki baaki kaanoonon ke tahat 15 din kii remand hi milti he
 Apart from this, there will be a provision of five years of imprisonment and maximum of the death sentence for the offender

 In such a situation there was no need to bring UPCOCA, because there is a possibility of misuse of it

 Also, a monolithic flame that burns for nine days is also lit
 ghat sthapanakarte samay yadi kuch niyamon kaa paalan bhi kiya jaae to or bhi shubh hota he
 Mothers are very happy to follow these rules
 navaratri main kaise karen kalash sthapana (kalash Sthapana Vidhi in Navratri)agar aap ghar main kalash sthapana kar rahe hai to sabase pehle kalash par swaastik banaaen
 Then tie a molly on the urn and fill it with water
 kalash main sabut supaari, phool, itr or panchratra va sikaa daalen
 Put it intact as well
 kalash sthapana hameshaa shubh muhoort main kerani chahie
 Meditate after daily work and bath
 iske baad pujan sthal se alag ek pate par laal va safed kapadaa bichhaaen
 On this, make an octopus from Akshat and install an urn filled with water on it
 kalash kaa munh khulaa naa rakhen, use kisi cheez se dhak dena chahie
 If the urn is covered with a lid, fill it with rice and keep a coconut in the middle
 is kalash main shatavari jadi, halkund, camel gatta va rajat kaa sikaa daalen
 Light the lamp and meditate on the deity
 tatpashchaat devi mantra kaa jaap karen
 Now plant wheat and barley in earthen pot in front of the urn
 is jware ko mataji kaa swaroop maanakar pujan karen
 Immerse the sorghum on the last day
 kalash sthapana kii sahi disha-1
 Ishaan angle (north-east) is considered to be the direction of the deities
 isi disha main mata kii pratimaa tathaa ghat sthapana karnaa uchit rahata he
 2
 mata pratimaa ke saamne akhand jyoti jalaaen to use aagney kone (purv-dakshin) main rakhen
 While performing the puja keep the mouth in the east or north direction
 3
 It is auspicious if you do the installation on sandal wood
 puja sthal ke aas-paas gandagi nahin honi chahie
 4
 kai log navaratri main dhwaja bhi badalte hai
 Establish the flag on the roof of the house in an aerial angle (northwest)
 5
 a little space should be open in front of the place of worship, where meditation and reading etc
 can be done
 6
 There should not be toilets or bathrooms around the installation site
 puja sthal ke upar yadi taand ho to use saafe-suthri rakhen

 balki kisi ko khabar na ho, kahin tasviir na aae, isliye vahaan ke logon ke phone or bank main lage camere bhi lut le gaye

 The central government said on Tuesday that 17 new mega food parks have been approved
 khaadya prasanskaran udyog mantralay ke mutabik mantralay ko 72 prastaav mili hai or in par paardarshee dhang se gaur karne ke baad desh ke 11 rajyon ke 17 samuchit prastaavon kaa chayan kiya gaya he or un par amal ke liye manjuuri bhi de di gai he
 The statement said that so far 42 mega food parks have been approved by the government to set up across the country
 maujuuda samay main 25 pariyojnaayen nimarnadhin hai
 This move of the government will create huge state-of-the-art infrastructure for the food processing sector and give a new impetus to the development of this sector
 in 17 nae mega food parkon se atyaadhunik buniyadi dhaanche main takreeban 2000 karod rupee kaa nivesh aakarshith hone kaa anumaan he
 Similarly, in the 500 food processing units located in the parks, an additional collective investment of about Rs 4,000 crore is expected to be attracted
 inkaa salanaa kaarobaar 8,000 karod rupee rahane kaa anumaan lagaaya gaya he
 Once these parks are fully functional, employment will be created for about 80,000 people and about 5 lakh farmers will be benefited directly and indirectly
 bayaan ke mutabik in mega food parkon ke samay par puraa ho jane se sambandhit rajyon main khaadya prasanskaran kshetra ke vikaas ko badhaava milegaa, kisaanon ko behatar mulya milane main madad milegi, jald kharaab hone vaale khaadya padaarthon kii barbaadi ghategi, krishi upaj kaa moolyavardhan hoga or khaskar gramin kshetron main badi sankhya main rojgaar avasar srujit honge
 Not only this, these mega food parks will help in keeping the prices of food products stable as well as in keeping inflation under control in the country
